<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-109"><dt><span id="must_specify__c_ext_for_abstract_declarators"></span><span id="MUST_SPECIFY__C_EXT_FOR_ABSTRACT_DECLARATORS"></span>必須為抽象宣告子指定/c_ext</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-109"><dt><span id="must_specify__c_ext_for_abstract_declarators"></span><span id="MUST_SPECIFY__C_EXT_FOR_ABSTRACT_DECLARATORS"></span>must specify /c_ext for abstract declarators</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-110">抽象宣告子代表 Microsoft 對 RPC 的延伸模組，而且不會在 DCE RPC 中定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-110">Abstract declarators represent a Microsoft extension to RPC and are not defined in DCE RPC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-111">因此，如果您的檔案包含抽象宣告子，您就無法使用 <a href="-osf.md"><strong>/osf</strong></a> 參數進行編譯，這會強制執行嚴格的 DCE 相容性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-111">Therefore, if your file includes abstract declarators, you cannot compile with the <a href="-osf.md"><strong>/osf</strong></a> switch, which enforces strict DCE compatibility.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-112">MIDL 3.0 版和更新版本會使用 <a href="-c-ext.md"><strong>/c_ext</strong></a> 參數作為預設值; <strong>/osf</strong> 參數會關閉 <strong>/c_ext</strong> 參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-112">MIDL versions 3.0 and later use the <a href="-c-ext.md"><strong>/c_ext</strong></a> switch as the default; the <strong>/osf</strong> switch turns off the <strong>/c_ext</strong> switch.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-113">如需抽象宣告子的詳細資訊，請參閱 <a href="/windows/desktop/Rpc/the-acf-body">ACF 主體</a>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-113">For information on abstract declarators, see <a href="/windows/desktop/Rpc/the-acf-body">The ACF Body</a>.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>

id="NO__POINTER_DEFAULT__ATTRIBUTE_SPECIFIED__ASSUMING__UNIQUE__FOR_ALL_UNATTRIBUTED_POINTERS"></span>未指定 [pointer_default] 屬性，假設 [unique] 適用于所有未歸屬指標</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-258"><dt><span id="no__pointer_default__attribute_specified__assuming__unique__for_all_unattributed_pointers"></span><span id="NO__POINTER_DEFAULT__ATTRIBUTE_SPECIFIED__ASSUMING__UNIQUE__FOR_ALL_UNATTRIBUTED_POINTERS"></span>no [pointer_default] attribute specified, assuming [unique] for all unattributed pointers</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-259">MIDL 編譯器針對沒有指標屬性的指標提供三種不同的預設案例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-259">The MIDL compiler offers three different default cases for data-ttu-id="ced98-262">當未提供 [<strong>pointer_default</strong>] 屬性時，這些 nontop 層級指標會預設為唯一指標。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-262">When no [<strong>pointer_default</strong>] {
    short x;

<td><span id="MIDL2085"></span><span id="midl2085"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-441"><dt><strong>MIDL2085</strong></dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-441"><dt><strong>MIDL2085</strong></dt> </span></span></dl></td>
<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-442"><dt><span id="_transmit_as__must_specify_a_transmissible_type"></span><span id="_TRANSMIT_AS__MUST_SPECIFY_A_TRANSMISSIBLE_TYPE"></span>[transmit_as] 必須指定 transmissible 類型</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-442"><dt><span id="_transmit_as__must_specify_a_transmissible_type"></span><span id="_TRANSMIT_AS__MUST_SPECIFY_A_TRANSMISSIBLE_TYPE"></span>[transmit_as] must specify a transmissible type</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-443">指定的 [<a href="transmit-as.md"><strong>transmit_as</strong></a>] 類型衍生自無法由 Microsoft RPC 傳送的類型，例如 <a href="void.md"><strong>void</strong></a>、 <strong>void \*</strong>或 <a href="int.md"><strong>int</strong></a>。使用已定義的 RPC 基底類型;如果是 <strong>int</strong>，請新增大小規範（例如 <a href="small.md"><strong>small</strong></a>、 <a href="short.md"><strong>short</strong></a>或 <a href="long.md"><strong>long</strong></a> ）來限定 <strong>int</strong>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-443">The specified [<a href="transmit-as.md"><strong>transmit_as</strong></a>] type derives from a type that cannot be transmitted by Microsoft RPC, such as <a href="void.md"><strong>void</strong></a>, <strong>void \*</strong>, or <a href="int.md"><strong>int</strong></a>. Use a defined RPC base type; in the case of <strong>int</strong>, add size specifiers like <a href="small.md"><strong>small</strong></a>, <a href="short.md"><strong>short</strong></a>, or <a href="long.md"><strong>long</strong></a> to qualify the <strong>int</strong>.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>
</tr>

<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-709"><dt><span id="_allocate__attribute_must_be_applied_only_on_non-void_pointer_types"></span><span id="_ALLOCATE__ATTRIBUTE_MUST_BE_APPLIED_ONLY_ON_NON-VOID_POINTER_TYPES"></span>[配置] 屬性必須只套用在非 void 指標類型上</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-709"><dt><span id="_allocate__attribute_must_be_applied_only_on_non-void_pointer_types"></span><span id="_ALLOCATE__ATTRIBUTE_MUST_BE_APPLIED_ONLY_ON_NON-VOID_POINTER_TYPES"></span>[allocate] attribute must be applied only on non-void pointer types</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-710">[<a href="allocate.md"><strong>配置</strong></a>] 屬性是針對複雜的以指標為基礎的資料結構所設計。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-710">The [<a href="allocate.md"><strong>allocate</strong></a>] attribute is designed for complex pointer-based data structures.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-711">當指定 [配置] 屬性時，存根檔會遍歷資料結構，以計算所有可從指標存取的所有物件的總大小，以及資料結構中的所有其他指標。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-711">When the [allocate] attribute is specified, the stub file traverses the data structure to compute the total size of all objects accessible from the pointer and all other pointers in the data structure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-712">將類型變更為 void 指標類型或移除 [<strong>配置</strong>] 屬性，並使用另一個方法來判斷其配置大小，例如 <strong>sizeof</strong> 運算子。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-712">Change the type to a nonvoid pointer type or remove the [<strong>allocate</strong>] attribute and use another method to determine its allocation size, such as the <strong>sizeof</strong> operator.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>

<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-727"><dt><span id="parameter_or_return_value_must_not_derive_from_a_type_that_has__ignore__applied_to_it"></span><span id="PARAMETER_OR_RETURN_VALUE_MUST_NOT_DERIVE_FROM_A_TYPE_THAT_HAS__IGNORE__APPLIED_TO_IT"></span>參數或傳回值不能衍生自已套用 [ignore] 的類型</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-727"><dt><span id="parameter_or_return_value_must_not_derive_from_a_type_that_has__ignore__applied_to_it"></span><span id="PARAMETER_OR_RETURN_VALUE_MUST_NOT_DERIVE_FROM_A_TYPE_THAT_HAS__IGNORE__APPLIED_TO_IT"></span>parameter or return value must not derive from a type that has [ignore] applied to it</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-728">[<a href="ignore.md"><strong>忽略</strong></a>] 屬性是只能套用至欄位（例如結構和陣列的欄位）的欄位屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-728">The [<a href="ignore.md"><strong>ignore</strong></a>] attribute is a field attribute that can be applied only to fields, such as fields of structures and arrays.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-729">[<strong>Ignore</strong>] 屬性工作表示存根不應該在傳輸期間對指標進行取值，而且當它與必須取值的其他屬性（例如 [<a href="out-idl.md"><strong>out</strong></a>] 參數和函式傳回值）衝突時，就不能使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-729">The [<strong>ignore</strong>] attribute indicates that the stub should not dereference the pointer during transmission and is not allowed when it conflicts with other attributes that must be dereferenced, such as [<a href="out-idl.md"><strong>out</strong></a>] parameters and function return values.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>
</tr>

<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-734"><dt><span id="field_parameter_must_not_derive_from_a_structure_that_is_recursive_through_a_ref_pointer"></span><span id="FIELD_PARAMETER_MUST_NOT_DERIVE_FROM_A_STRUCTURE_THAT_IS_RECURSIVE_THROUGH_A_REF_POINTER"></span>field/parameter 不能衍生自透過 ref 指標遞迴的結構</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-734"><dt><span id="field_parameter_must_not_derive_from_a_structure_that_is_recursive_through_a_ref_pointer"></span><span id="FIELD_PARAMETER_MUST_NOT_DERIVE_FROM_A_STRUCTURE_THAT_IS_RECURSIVE_THROUGH_A_REF_POINTER"></span>field/parameter must not derive from a structure that is recursive through a ref pointer</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-735">根據定義，參考指標不能設定為 <strong>Null</strong>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-735">By definition, a reference pointer cannot be set to <strong>NULL</strong>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-736">使用參考指標定義的遞迴資料結構沒有 <strong>Null</strong> 元素，而且依慣例為非終止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-736">A recursive data structure defined with a reference pointer has no <strong>NULL</strong> elements and by convention is nonterminating.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-737">您可以使用 [<a href="unique.md"><strong>unique</strong></a>] 指標屬性，讓資料結構指定 <strong>Null</strong> 元素，或將資料結構重新定義為非遞迴資料結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-737">Use a [<a href="unique.md"><strong>unique</strong></a>] pointer attribute to allow the data structure to specify a <strong>NULL</strong> element, or redefine the data structure as a nonrecursive data structure.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>

<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-768"><dt><span id="no__pointer_default__attribute_specified__assuming__ptr__for_all_unattributed_pointers_in_interface"></span><span id="NO__POINTER_DEFAULT__ATTRIBUTE_SPECIFIED__ASSUMING__PTR__FOR_ALL_UNATTRIBUTED_POINTERS_IN_INTERFACE"></span>未指定 [pointer_default] 屬性，假設 [ptr] 針對介面中的所有未歸屬指標</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-768"><dt><span id="no__pointer_default__attribute_specified__assuming__ptr__for_all_unattributed_pointers_in_interface"></span><span id="NO__POINTER_DEFAULT__ATTRIBUTE_SPECIFIED__ASSUMING__PTR__FOR_ALL_UNATTRIBUTED_POINTERS_IN_INTERFACE"></span>no [pointer_default] attribute specified, assuming [ptr] for all unattributed pointers in interface</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-769">「DCE IDL」實指定每個 IDL 檔案中的所有指標都必須與指標屬性相關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-769">The DCE IDL implementation specifies that all pointers in each IDL file must be associated with pointer attributes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-770">如果未將明確指標屬性指派給參數或指標類型，而且在 IDL 檔案中未指定任何 [<a the pointer attributes by using explicit pointer attributes, by specifying a [<strong>pointer_default</strong>] attribute, or by specifying the <a href="-ms-ext.md"><strong>/ms_ext</strong></a> switch to change the default for unattributed pointers to [<a href="unique.md"><strong>unique</strong></a>].</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>

<td><span id="MIDL2369"></span><span id="midl2369"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1476"><dt><strong>MIDL2369</strong></dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1476"><dt><strong>MIDL2369</strong></dt> </span></span></dl></td>
<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1477"><dt><span id="exceeded_stack_size_for__Oi__using__Os"></span><span id="exceeded_stack_size_for__oi__using__os"></span><span id="EXCEEDED_STACK_SIZE_FOR__OI__USING__OS"></span>使用/Os 超過/Oi 的堆疊大小</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1477"><dt><span id="exceeded_stack_size_for__Oi__using__Os"></span><span id="exceeded_stack_size_for__oi__using__os"></span><span id="EXCEEDED_STACK_SIZE_FOR__OI__USING__OS"></span>exceeded stack size for /Oi, using /Os</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1478">-Oi 優化模式的參數限制為128個位元組的堆疊空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1478">The -Oi optimization mode is limited to 128 bytes of stack space for parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1479">編譯器已自動切換至 Os 優化模式，以解決這項限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1479">The compiler has automatically switched to the Os optimization mode to work around this limitation.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1480">若要避免這個警告，請使用-Oicf 或-Os 優化模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1480">To avoid this warning, use the -Oicf or -Os optimization modes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1481">您可以在命令列上變更優化模式，方法是指定-Oicf 或-Os，而不是-Oi，或在 ACF 檔案中新增 [optimize9 &quot; icf &quot;) ] 或將 [ (&quot; s &quot;) ] 屬性優化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1481">The optimization mode may be changed on the command line by specifying -Oicf or -Os instead of -Oi or by adding an [optimize9&quot;icf&quot;)] or optimize[(&quot;s&quot;)] attribute to the function in the ACF file.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1482">當以傳值方式將大型結構傳遞為參數時，通常會發生這個警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1482">This warning typically happens when passing large structures as parameters by value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1483">您可以改為傳遞結構的指標，來降低所需的堆疊大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1483">The required stack size can be lowered by passing a pointer to the structure instead.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1484">範例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1484">Example:</span></span><br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>typedef struct
{
char a[127];
}
large;
//This function has a stack size of 132 (x86) or 136 (alpha) on 32-bit systems
void roo(large s, int a);    //MIDL 2360
// workaround: pass by reference
void bar (large *s, int a);</code></pre>
</dd> </dl></td>
</tr>

icf &quot;) </strong>] 屬性新增至 ACF 檔案中的函式，來變更個別函式的優化模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1569">The optimization mode can be changed for an individual function by adding the [<strong>optimize(&quot;icf&quot;)</strong>] attribute to the function in the ACF file.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1570">下列範例示範此警告：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1570">The following example demonstrates this warning:</span></span><br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>void roo(long s1, [size_is(s1)] long a[][30];    //MIDL2393
void bar(long s1, long s2, [size_is(s1,s2) long **a);//MIDL2393</code></pre>

<td><span id="MIDL2395"></span><span id="midl2395"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1571"><dt><strong>MIDL2395</strong></dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1571"><dt><strong>MIDL2395</strong></dt> </span></span></dl></td>
<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1572"><dt><span id="type_or_construct_not_supported_in_a_library_block_because_Oleaut32.dll_support_for_64-KB_polymorphic_types_is_missing"></span><span id="type_or_construct_not_supported_in_a_library_block_because_oleaut32.dll_support_for_64-kb_polymorphic_types_is_missing"></span><span id="TYPE_OR_CONSTRUCT_NOT_SUPPORTED_IN_A_LIBRARY_BLOCK_BECAUSE_OLEAUT32.DLL_SUPPORT_FOR_64-KB_POLYMORPHIC_TYPES_IS_MISSING"></span>程式庫區塊中不支援類型或結構，因為缺少 64-KB 多型類型的 Oleaut32.dll 支援</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1572"><dt><span id="type_or_construct_not_supported_in_a_library_block_because_Oleaut32.dll_support_for_64-KB_polymorphic_types_is_missing"></span><span id="type_or_construct_not_supported_in_a_library_block_because_oleaut32.dll_support_for_64-kb_polymorphic_types_is_missing"></span><span id="TYPE_OR_CONSTRUCT_NOT_SUPPORTED_IN_A_LIBRARY_BLOCK_BECAUSE_OLEAUT32.DLL_SUPPORT_FOR_64-KB_POLYMORPHIC_TYPES_IS_MISSING"></span>type or construct not supported in a library block because Oleaut32.dll support for 64-KB polymorphic types is missing</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1573">OLE automation 不支援多型類型 (例如 _int3264、INT_PTR 等) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1573">OLE automation does not support polymorphic types (such as _int3264, INT_PTR, etc).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1574">這些類型在32位和64位平臺之間具有不相容的資料標記法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1574">These types have incompatible data representations between 32-bit and 64-bit platforms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1575">在64位平臺上，遠端呼叫會在執行時間失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1575">The remote call will fail at run time on 64-bit platforms.</span></span><br/>
<blockquote>
[!Note]<br />
<span data-ttu-id="ced98-1576">請注意，在 Windows 2000 版本中，OLE Automation 會在執行時間轉換32位 TLB 資訊，以支援64位 TLB 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1576">Note that as of Windows 2000 release, 64-bit TLB files are supported by OLE Automation by converting 32-bit TLB information at run time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1577">因此，MIDL 只支援32位的 TLB 產生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1577">Therefore, only 32-bit TLB generation is supported by MIDL.</span></span>
</blockquote>
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1578">如果使用 MIDL 來產生標頭檔， <a href="-notlb.md"><strong>/notlb</strong></a> 參數將會抑制 TLB 檔案的產生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1578">If MIDL is being used just to generate a header file, the <a href="-notlb.md"><strong>/notlb</strong></a> switch will suppress generation of the TLB file.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>
</tr>

<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1643"><dt><span id="internal_compiler_inconsistency_detected__the_format_string_offset_is_invalid._See_the_documentation_for_more_information."></span><span id="internal_compiler_inconsistency_detected__the_format_string_offset_is_invalid._see_the_documentation_for_more_information."></span><span id="INTERNAL_COMPILER_INCONSISTENCY_DETECTED__THE_FORMAT_STRING_OFFSET_IS_INVALID._SEE_THE_DOCUMENTATION_FOR_MORE_INFORMATION."></span>偵測到內部編譯器不一致：格式字串位移無效。如需詳細資訊，請參閱檔。</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1643"><dt><span id="internal_compiler_inconsistency_detected__the_format_string_offset_is_invalid._See_the_documentation_for_more_information."></span><span id="internal_compiler_inconsistency_detected__the_format_string_offset_is_invalid._see_the_documentation_for_more_information."></span><span id="INTERNAL_COMPILER_INCONSISTENCY_DETECTED__THE_FORMAT_STRING_OFFSET_IS_INVALID._SEE_THE_DOCUMENTATION_FOR_MORE_INFORMATION."></span>internal compiler inconsistency detected: the format string offset is invalid. See the documentation for more information.</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1644">MIDL 編譯器偵測到其內部資料結構中的值無效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1644">The MIDL compiler detected an invalid value in its internal data structures.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1645">這可能是因為遞迴或編譯器違反本身內部資料的表示限制所造成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1645">This may be caused by structures that are recursive or by compiler breaching its own limits of representation for internal data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1646">若要找出及/或解決此問題，請嘗試簡化 IDL 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1646">To identify and/or work around the problem, try to simplify the IDL file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1647">若要這麼做，您可以簡化複雜的參數和遞迴資料結構，或藉由分割來使 IDL 檔案變得更小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1647">You can do this by simplifying complex parameters and recursive data structures or making the IDL file smaller by splitting it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1648">此訊息可能伴隨著診斷輸出，並提供問題的其他相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1648">This message may be accompanied by a diagnostic printout with additional information about the problem.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1649">如果您看到此錯誤，請向 Microsoft 回報錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1649">If you see this error, report a bug to Microsoft.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1650">指定 IDL 檔案、ACF 檔、完整 MIDL 命令列，以及診斷輸出（如果有的話）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1650">Specify your IDL files, ACF files, full MIDL command line, and diagnostic output, if any.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>

<td><span id="MIDL2414"></span><span id="midl2414"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1669"><dt><strong>MIDL2414</strong></dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1669"><dt><strong>MIDL2414</strong></dt> </span></span></dl></td>
<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1670"><dt><span id="floating_point_or_complex_return_types_with__decode__are_not_supported_in_-Oicf__using_-OI"></span><span id="floating_point_or_complex_return_types_with__decode__are_not_supported_in_-oicf__using_-oi"></span><span id="FLOATING_POINT_OR_COMPLEX_RETURN_TYPES_WITH__DECODE__ARE_NOT_SUPPORTED_IN_-OICF__USING_-OI"></span>使用-OI 的 Oicf 中不支援具有 [解碼] 的浮點或複雜傳回類型</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1670"><dt><span id="floating_point_or_complex_return_types_with__decode__are_not_supported_in_-Oicf__using_-OI"></span><span id="floating_point_or_complex_return_types_with__decode__are_not_supported_in_-oicf__using_-oi"></span><span id="FLOATING_POINT_OR_COMPLEX_RETURN_TYPES_WITH__DECODE__ARE_NOT_SUPPORTED_IN_-OICF__USING_-OI"></span>floating point or complex return types with [decode] are not supported in -Oicf, using -OI</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1671">Oicf 樣式 pickling 不支援具有浮點或結構/等位傳回類型的程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1671">Procedures with floating point or structure/union return types are not supported in the -Oicf style pickling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1672">32位的解決方式是在使用 [編碼] 和/或 [解碼] ) 序列化資料 (時，使用-Oi 優化模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1672">A work around for 32-bit is to use the -Oi optimization mode when serializing data (using [encode] and/or [decode]).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1673">不過，由於舊的 Oi 樣式解譯器和 pickling 支援已預定在 Windows 2000 版本之後淘汰，因此強烈建議您使用指標作為此問題的解決方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1673">However, as the old -Oi style interpreter and pickling support are slated to be phased out after the Windows 2000 release, using pointers is strongly suggested as the work around for this problem.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1674">另請注意，通常會將介面方法變更為使用 [out，ref] 指標，而不是傳回值，而導致問題在網路上完全相容，而且可以輕鬆地隱藏在應用層。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1674">Also note that typically, changing an interface method to use an [out, ref] pointer instead of the return value causing the problem is fully backward-compatible on wire and can be easily hidden from the app layer.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1675">在 MIDL 命令列上指定-Oi 或針對個別函式，藉由在 ACF 檔案的函式中新增 [optimize (&quot; i &quot;) ] 屬性，即可全域隱藏這個警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1675">This warning can be suppressed globally by specifying -Oi on the MIDL command line or for an individual function by adding the [optimize(&quot;i&quot;)] attribute to the function in the ACF file.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1676">下列範例示範此問題：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1676">The following example demonstrates the issue:</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1677">roo .idl：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1677">roo.idl:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>double GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="ced98-1678">roo. acf：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1678">roo.acf:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>[decode] GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="ced98-1679">解決這項限制的其中一個方法是傳遞 [out] 參數來保存結果，而不是使用傳回值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1679">One option to work around this limitation would be to pass an [out] parameter to hold the result instead of using a return value:</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1680">roo .idl：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1680">roo.idl:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>void GetDouble([out] double *result); //top level pointer is a [ref] pointer</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="ced98-1681">roo. acf：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1681">roo.acf:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>[decode] GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="ced98-1682">如先前所述，上述解決方案不只適用于新介面，也適用于舊介面的解決方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1682">As mentioned earlier, the solution described above is good not only for the new interfaces but also as a work-around for the old ones.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1683">新輸出引數的網路標記法與傳回 &quot; &quot; 值相同， (請注意 void 作為新的傳回值) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1683">The wire representation for the new &quot;out&quot; argument is the same as for the return value (notice void as the new return value).</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>
</tr>

<td><span id="MIDL2415"></span><span id="midl2415"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1684"><dt><strong>MIDL2415</strong></dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1684"><dt><strong>MIDL2415</strong></dt> </span></span></dl></td>
<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1685"><dt><span id="the_return_type_is_not_supported_for_64-bit_when_using__decode_"></span><span id="THE_RETURN_TYPE_IS_NOT_SUPPORTED_FOR_64-BIT_WHEN_USING__DECODE_"></span>使用 [解碼] 時，64位不支援傳回類型</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1685"><dt><span id="the_return_type_is_not_supported_for_64-bit_when_using__decode_"></span><span id="THE_RETURN_TYPE_IS_NOT_SUPPORTED_FOR_64-BIT_WHEN_USING__DECODE_"></span>the return type is not supported for 64-bit when using [decode]</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1686">使用 [ <a href="encode.md"><strong>編碼</strong></a> <a href="decode.md"><strong>] 和/或 [解碼</strong></a>] ) 執行資料序列化 (時，64位模式不支援具有浮點或結構/等位傳回類型的程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1686">Procedures with floating point or structure/union return types are not supported in 64-bit mode when performing data serialization (using [ <a href="encode.md"><strong>encode</strong></a>] and/or [ <a href="decode.md"><strong>decode</strong></a>]).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1687">這與舊版樣式-Oi 解譯器和64位平臺上不支援的資料序列化程式有關。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1687">This is related to the old style -Oi interpreter and data serializer not being supported on 64-bit platform.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1688">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 MIDL2414 的描述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1688">Please see the description of MIDL2414 for more information.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1689">下列範例示範此錯誤：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1689">The following example demonstrates this error:</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1690">roo .idl：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1690">roo.idl:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>double GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="ced98-1691">roo. acf：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1691">roo.acf:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>[decode] GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="ced98-1692">建議您將下列各項作為新舊介面的解決方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1692">The following is advised as a work-around for both new and old interfaces.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1693">使用 [out] 參數來保存結果，而不是使用傳回值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1693">Use an [out] parameter to hold the result instead of using a return value:</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1694">roo .idl：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1694">roo.idl:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>void GetDouble([out] double *result); //top level pointer is a [ref] pointer.</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="ced98-1695">roo. acf：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1695">roo.acf:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>[decode] GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="ced98-1696">請注意，在網路上，此解決方案完全是回溯相容的，因為 [ref，out] 指標或雙精度的網路標記法與雙精度相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1696">Note that this solution is fully backward-compatible on wire, as the wire representation of a [ref, out] pointer or a double is the same as that of a double.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>
</tr>
<tr class="even">
<td><span id="MIDL2416"></span><span id="midl2416"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1697"><dt><strong>MIDL2416</strong></dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1697"><dt><strong>MIDL2416</strong></dt> </span></span></dl></td>
<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1698"><dt><span id="transmitted_type_may_not_contain_a_full_pointer_for_either__wire_marshal__or__user_marshal_"></span><span id="TRANSMITTED_TYPE_MAY_NOT_CONTAIN_A_FULL_POINTER_FOR_EITHER__WIRE_MARSHAL__OR__USER_MARSHAL_"></span>傳送的型別不能包含 [wire_marshal] 或 [user_marshal] 的完整指標</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1698"><dt><span id="transmitted_type_may_not_contain_a_full_pointer_for_either__wire_marshal__or__user_marshal_"></span><span id="TRANSMITTED_TYPE_MAY_NOT_CONTAIN_A_FULL_POINTER_FOR_EITHER__WIRE_MARSHAL__OR__USER_MARSHAL_"></span>transmitted type may not contain a full pointer for either [wire_marshal] or [user_marshal]</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1699">具有 [ <a href="wire-marshal.md"><strong>wire_marshal</strong></a>] 或 [ <a href="user-marshal.md"><strong>user_marshal</strong></a>] 屬性的類型，不能包含完整的 ( [ <strong>ptr</strong>] ) 指標。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1699">Types with [ <a href="wire-marshal.md"><strong>wire_marshal</strong></a>] or [ <a href="user-marshal.md"><strong>user_marshal</strong></a>] attributes may not contain full ([ <strong>ptr</strong>]) pointers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1700">請改用 [ <a href="unique.md"><strong>unique</strong></a>] 或 [ <a href="ref.md"><strong>ref</strong></a>]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1700">Use [ <a href="unique.md"><strong>unique</strong></a>] or [ <a href="ref.md"><strong>ref</strong></a>] instead.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1701">下列範例示範此錯誤：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1701">The following example demonstrates this error:</span></span><br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>typedef struct
{
    [ptr] long *a;    //Should use [ref] or [unique] instead
}
st1;
typedef [wire_marshal(st1)] struct
{
    long a;
}
st2:
void roo(st2 *s);    //MIDL2416</code></pre>
</dd> </dl></td>
</tr>

<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1703"><dt><span id="transmitted_type_must_either_be_a_pointer_or_have_a_constant_size_for__wire_marshal__and__user_marshal_"></span><span id="TRANSMITTED_TYPE_MUST_EITHER_BE_A_POINTER_OR_HAVE_A_CONSTANT_SIZE_FOR__WIRE_MARSHAL__AND__USER_MARSHAL_"></span>傳輸的類型必須是指標，或具有 [wire_marshal] 和 [user_marshal] 的常數大小</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1703"><dt><span id="transmitted_type_must_either_be_a_pointer_or_have_a_constant_size_for__wire_marshal__and__user_marshal_"></span><span id="TRANSMITTED_TYPE_MUST_EITHER_BE_A_POINTER_OR_HAVE_A_CONSTANT_SIZE_FOR__WIRE_MARSHAL__AND__USER_MARSHAL_"></span>transmitted type must either be a pointer or have a constant size for [wire_marshal] and [user_marshal]</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1704">具有 [ <a href="wire-marshal.md"><strong>wire_marshal</strong></a>] 或 [ <a href="user-marshal.md"><strong>user_marshal</strong></a>] 屬性的最上層類型，在編譯時期必須有妥善定義的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1704">Top-level types with [ <a href="wire-marshal.md"><strong>wire_marshal</strong></a>] or [ <a href="user-marshal.md"><strong>user_marshal</strong></a>] attributes must have a well-defined size at compile time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1705">它們不能是或包含一致或不同大小的陣列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1705">They cannot be or contain conformant or varying-sized arrays.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1706">下列範例示範此錯誤：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1706">The following example demonstrates this error:</span></span><br/>

{
    long s;
    [size_is(s)] char a[];
}
st1;
typedef [wire_marshal(st1)] struct
{
    long a;
}
st2;
void roo(st2 *s);        //MIDL2417</code></pre>
</dd> </dl></td>

{
    long s;
    [size_is(s)] char a[];
}
st1;
void roo(st1 s);        //MIDL2465
 
on .acf file

<tr class="odd">
<td><span id="MIDL9008"></span><span id="midl9008"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1721"><dt><strong>MIDL9008</strong></dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1721"><dt><strong>MIDL9008</strong></dt> </span></span></dl></td>
<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1722"><dt><span id="_internal_compiler_problem__system_error_code__-_the_compiler_cannot_continue_for_an_unknown_reason._See_documentation_for_a_workaround."></span><span id="_internal_compiler_problem__system_error_code__-_the_compiler_cannot_continue_for_an_unknown_reason._see_documentation_for_a_workaround."></span><span id="_INTERNAL_COMPILER_PROBLEM__SYSTEM_ERROR_CODE__-_THE_COMPILER_CANNOT_CONTINUE_FOR_AN_UNKNOWN_REASON._SEE_DOCUMENTATION_FOR_A_WORKAROUND."></span> 編譯器內部問題 <system error code> - ：編譯器無法繼續，原因不明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1722"><dt><span id="_internal_compiler_problem__system_error_code__-_the_compiler_cannot_continue_for_an_unknown_reason._See_documentation_for_a_workaround."></span><span id="_internal_compiler_problem__system_error_code__-_the_compiler_cannot_continue_for_an_unknown_reason._see_documentation_for_a_workaround."></span><span id="_INTERNAL_COMPILER_PROBLEM__SYSTEM_ERROR_CODE__-_THE_COMPILER_CANNOT_CONTINUE_FOR_AN_UNKNOWN_REASON._SEE_DOCUMENTATION_FOR_A_WORKAROUND."></span> internal compiler problem <system error code> - the compiler cannot continue for an unknown reason.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1723">請參閱檔以瞭解因應措施。</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1723">See documentation for a workaround.</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1724">編譯器無法繼續，且錯誤的原因不明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1724">The compiler could not continue and the cause of the error is unknown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1725">十六進位錯誤號碼是系統錯誤識別碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1725">The hexadecimal error number is a system-error identifier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1726">編譯可能因為外部問題而失敗，例如記憶體不足的狀況。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1726">The compile may have failed because of an external problem, such as an out-of-memory condition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1727">在這種情況下，您可以在 Winerror.h 中找到詳細資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1727">In that case, you can find more information in Winerror.h or Ntstatus.h.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1728">有兩種情況通常會產生此錯誤：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1728">There are two situations that usually generate this error:</span></span><br/>
<ul>
<li><span data-ttu-id="ced98-1729">在 IDL 檔案中偵測到錯誤之後，MIDL 編譯器無法復原。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1729">The MIDL compiler failed to recover after detecting an error in the IDL file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1730">如果 MIDL 傳回任何關於 IDL 檔案的錯誤訊息，請嘗試修正它們並重新編譯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1730">If MIDL returned any error messages about your IDL file, try fixing them and recompiling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1731">如果沒有任何錯誤訊息，編譯器可能會在報告錯誤之前失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1731">If there are no error messages, the compiler may have failed before it could report an error.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1732">在報告內部編譯器錯誤的行上尋找語法錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1732">Look for a syntax error on the line for which the internal compiler error is reported.</span></span></li>
<li><span data-ttu-id="ced98-1733">MIDL 編譯器無法在指定的優化選項下產生正確的程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1733">The MIDL compiler could not generate correct code under a specified optimization option.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1734">請嘗試變更編譯器模式、在混合模式優化 (/<a href="-os.md"><strong>Os</strong></a>) 中進行編譯，或移除所有優化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1734">Try changing compiler modes, compiling in mixed-mode optimization (/<a href="-os.md"><strong>Os</strong></a>), or removing all optimizations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1735">或者，使用/NO_FORMAT_OPT 旗標來重新編譯，以抑制 MIDL 的程式和類型描述元的預設優化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1735">Or, recompile using the /NO_FORMAT_OPT flag to suppress MIDL's default optimization of procedure and type descriptors.</span></span></li>
</ul>
<span data-ttu-id="ced98-1736">偶而發生此錯誤的原因是 IDL 檔案正確，且未使用任何優化選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1736">Occasionally this error occurs even when the IDL file is correct and no optimization options are being used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1737">如果發生這種情況，請嘗試藉由移除任何最近的修改、簡化或重新排列資料類型、變更原型，或開始將 IDL 檔案的部分標記為批註，以找出問題代碼，以重寫報告錯誤的區域中的程式碼區段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1737">If this is the case, try rewriting the section of code in the vicinity of where the error was reported by removing any recent modifications, simplifying or rearranging data types, changing prototypes, or else begin to comment out portions of the IDL file to locate the problem code.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="ced98-1738">如果這些選項都無法運作，或是您認為問題可能與 Midl.exe 中的錯誤有關，請通知 Microsoft，提供所有相關的詳細資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ced98-1738">If none of these options works, or if you think the problem may be related to a bug in Midl.exe, please notify Microsoft, giving all the relevant details.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>
</tr>
